\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
C\+A\+Nopen Service Data Object -\/ server protocol.

Service data objects (S\+D\+Os) allow the access to any entry of the C\+A\+Nopen Object dictionary. An S\+DO establishes a peer-\/to-\/peer communication channel between two devices. In addition, the S\+DO protocol enables to transfer any amount of data in a segmented way. Therefore the S\+DO protocol is mainly used in order to communicate configuration data.

All C\+A\+Nopen devices must have implemented S\+DO server and first S\+DO server channel. Servers serves data from Object dictionary. Object dictionary is a collection of variables, arrays or records (structures), which can be used by the stack or by the application. This file (C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O.\+h) implements S\+DO server.

S\+DO client can be (optionally) implemented on one (or multiple, if multiple S\+DO channels are used) device in C\+A\+Nopen network. Usually this is master device and provides also some kind of user interface, so configuration of the network is possible. Code for the S\+DO client is in file C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+Omaster.\+h.

S\+DO communication cycle is initiated by the client. Client can upload (read) data from device or can download (write) data to device. If data are less or equal of 4 bytes long, communication is finished by one server response (expedited transfer). If data are longer, they are split into multiple segments of request/response pairs (normal or segmented transfer). For longer data there is also a block transfer protocol, which transfers larger block of data in secure way with little protocol overhead. If error occurs during S\+DO transfer \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga7587ddcf798747fe6d97d03bf1bf2979}{C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+abort\+Code\+\_\+t}} is send by client or server and transfer is terminated.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga93b6bae3c759f44efab5ceeae57d4ac4}\label{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga93b6bae3c759f44efab5ceeae57d4ac4}} 
\index{SDO server@{SDO server}!CO\_SDO\_BUFFER\_SIZE@{CO\_SDO\_BUFFER\_SIZE}}
\index{CO\_SDO\_BUFFER\_SIZE@{CO\_SDO\_BUFFER\_SIZE}!SDO server@{SDO server}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CO\_SDO\_BUFFER\_SIZE}{CO\_SDO\_BUFFER\_SIZE}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE~32}

S\+DO buffer size.

Size of the internal S\+DO buffer.

Size must be at least equal to size of largest variable in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o__object_dictionary}{Object dictionary}}. If data type is domain, data length is not limited to S\+DO buffer size. If block transfer is implemented, value should be set to 889.

Value can be in range from 7 to 889 bytes.

\index{CO\_SDO\_OD\_flags\_t@{CO\_SDO\_OD\_flags\_t}!SDO server@{SDO server}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CO\_SDO\_OD\_flags\_t}{CO\_SDO\_OD\_flags\_t}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga954a22b6af836082afaf69b0f0cc4c7e}{C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+flags\+\_\+t}}}

Bit masks for flags associated with variable from \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o__object_dictionary}{Object dictionary}}.

This additional functionality of any variable in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o__object_dictionary}{Object dictionary}} can be enabled by function \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_gab433430abe125bb16c08e7be3e034985}{C\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+configure()}}. Location of the flag byte can be get from function \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga197661bebb5c451b3f4588fe1604f77d}{C\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+get\+Flags\+Pointer()}}. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CO\_ODFL\_RPDO\_WRITTEN@{CO\_ODFL\_RPDO\_WRITTEN}!SDO server@{SDO server}}\index{SDO server@{SDO server}!CO\_ODFL\_RPDO\_WRITTEN@{CO\_ODFL\_RPDO\_WRITTEN}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group___c_o___s_d_o_gga954a22b6af836082afaf69b0f0cc4c7eab6ffa5b9c34eabbe123e527ea274002f}\label{group___c_o___s_d_o_gga954a22b6af836082afaf69b0f0cc4c7eab6ffa5b9c34eabbe123e527ea274002f}} 
C\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+F\+L\+\_\+\+R\+P\+D\+O\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+T\+T\+EN&Variable was written by R\+P\+DO. Flag can be cleared by application \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CO\_ODFL\_TPDO\_MAPPED@{CO\_ODFL\_TPDO\_MAPPED}!SDO server@{SDO server}}\index{SDO server@{SDO server}!CO\_ODFL\_TPDO\_MAPPED@{CO\_ODFL\_TPDO\_MAPPED}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group___c_o___s_d_o_gga954a22b6af836082afaf69b0f0cc4c7eadc263192604b49113d0f522db5193ac5}\label{group___c_o___s_d_o_gga954a22b6af836082afaf69b0f0cc4c7eadc263192604b49113d0f522db5193ac5}} 
C\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+F\+L\+\_\+\+T\+P\+D\+O\+\_\+\+M\+A\+P\+P\+ED&Variable is mapped to T\+P\+DO \\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CO\_SDO\_OD\_flags\_t}{CO\_SDO\_OD\_flags\_t}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga954a22b6af836082afaf69b0f0cc4c7e}{C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+flags\+\_\+t}}}

Bit masks for flags associated with variable from \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o__object_dictionary}{Object dictionary}}.

This additional functionality of any variable in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o__object_dictionary}{Object dictionary}} can be enabled by function \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_gab433430abe125bb16c08e7be3e034985}{C\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+configure()}}. Location of the flag byte can be get from function \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga197661bebb5c451b3f4588fe1604f77d}{C\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+get\+Flags\+Pointer()}}. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CO\_OD\_configure()}{CO\_OD\_configure()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void C\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+configure (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_o___s_d_o__t}{C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{S\+DO,  }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{index,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga7587ddcf798747fe6d97d03bf1bf2979}{C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+abort\+Code\+\_\+t}}($\ast$)(\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_o___o_d_f__arg__t}{C\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+F\+\_\+arg\+\_\+t}} $\ast$O\+D\+F\+\_\+arg)}]{p\+O\+D\+Func,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{object,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{flags,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{flags\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Configure additional functionality to one \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o__object_dictionary}{Object dictionary}} entry.

Additional functionality include\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o___o_d__function}{Object Dictionary function}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga954a22b6af836082afaf69b0f0cc4c7e}{C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+flags\+\_\+t}}. It is optional feature and can be used on any object in Object dictionary. If OD entry does not exist, function returns silently.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em S\+DO} & This object. \\
\hline
{\em index} & Index of object in the Object dictionary. \\
\hline
{\em p\+O\+D\+Func} & Pointer to \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o___o_d__function}{Object Dictionary function}}, specified by application. If N\+U\+LL, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o___o_d__function}{Object Dictionary function}} will not be used on this object. \\
\hline
{\em object} & Pointer to object, which will be passed to \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o___o_d__function}{Object Dictionary function}}. \\
\hline
{\em flags} & Pointer to array of \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga954a22b6af836082afaf69b0f0cc4c7e}{C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+flags\+\_\+t}} defined externally. If zero, \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga954a22b6af836082afaf69b0f0cc4c7e}{C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+flags\+\_\+t}} will not be used on this OD entry. \\
\hline
{\em flags\+Size} & Size of the above array. It must be equal to number of sub-\/objects in object dictionary entry. Otherwise \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga954a22b6af836082afaf69b0f0cc4c7e}{C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+flags\+\_\+t}} will not be used on this OD entry. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Get attribute of the given object with specific sub\+Index. See \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o_ga0244f2d504e0de4f14614884d7319fd0}{C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+\+O\+D\+\_\+attributes\+\_\+t}}.

If Object Type is array and sub\+Index is zero, function always returns \textquotesingle{}read-\/only\textquotesingle{} attribute. An exception to this rule is I\+D1003 (Error field). However, this is supposed to be only written by network.

Initialize S\+DO object.

Function must be called in the communication reset section.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em S\+DO} & This object will be initialized. \\
\hline
{\em C\+O\+B\+\_\+\+I\+D\+Client\+To\+Server} & C\+OB ID for client to server for this S\+DO object. \\
\hline
{\em C\+O\+B\+\_\+\+I\+D\+Server\+To\+Client} & C\+OB ID for server to client for this S\+DO object. \\
\hline
{\em Obj\+Dict\+Index\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+Server\+Parameter} & Index in Object dictionary. \\
\hline
{\em parent\+S\+DO} & Pointer to S\+DO object, which contains object dictionary and its extension. For first (default) S\+DO object this argument must be N\+U\+LL. If this argument is specified, then OD, O\+D\+Size and O\+D\+Extensions arguments are ignored. \\
\hline
{\em OD} & Pointer to \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_o___s_d_o__object_dictionary}{Object dictionary}} array defined externally. \\
\hline
{\em O\+D\+Size} & Size of the above array. \\
\hline
{\em O\+D\+Extensions} & Pointer to the externally defined array of the same size as O\+D\+Size. \\
\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+init\+Callback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_o___s_d_o__t}{C\+O\+\_\+\+S\+D\+O\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{S\+DO,  }\item[{void($\ast$)(void)}]{p\+Funct\+Signal }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Initialize S\+D\+Orx callback function.

Function initializes optional callback function, which is called after new message is received from the C\+AN bus. Function may wake up external task, which processes mainline C\+A\+Nopen functions.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em S\+DO} & This object. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Funct\+Signal} & Pointer to the callback function. Not called if N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
